<text>My review is based on a togo order. The eatery is very upscale it they do not seem set up well for takeout orders.  The ramen and pork belly appetizer were delicious and packaged well for takeaway but the all the fried food I ordered was not packed well for take home. The leak-prof containers are air tight and trap in all the steam. I live 10 minutes away but the food would have been ruined as soon as the lid was closed. It is common sense to pack fried food in a container that is vented to let the steam out. I ordered 3 fried dishes at 8 dollars each so I wish the manager or chef would have been more knowledgeable about packaging fried food.< /text>< Pics>

Love the Marufuku in SF and so excited they're now in RWC. Ramen and appetizers are amazing. I've eaten there weekly since I found out they opened here, and quality is great every time. They package the food very carefully for takeout: broth, toppings, and noodles are kept separate. Service is very kind, and ramen is ready in less than 15 minutes after you call. Marufuku forever!!!!!!!!!<//Review>

<Resp>{'time': 1603837734343, 'text': 'Thank you for visiting our place.\nPlease come again. We will do our best every day to provide the same quality and the same service.\nWe look forward to seeing you again.\n\nThank you so mouch.'}<//Resp>< Review>
We came to the grand opening for Marufuku Ramen in Redwood City, and it's a great addition to the family of Marufuku restaurants! If you enjoy Marufuku in San Francisco or in Oakland, then you know to expect one of the best ramen spots in the Bay! As you walk in, you are greeted with some of the friendliest staff. The interior is elegantly decorated, and the outdoor provides plenty of space for a group setting. The food came out in less than 10 minutes and was the perfect temperature. We ordered the Hakata Tonkotsu and the Chicken Paitan DX. The broth for both ramen were phenomenal and the noodles were so fresh! The Chicken Paitan DX comes with a enormous piece of sizzling chicken so make sure you're hungry for that. All in all, the price was very reasonable for the amount of food you get. I can't wait to come here again!< /Review>

<text>I enjoyed a dare I say perfect lunch here! Upon arriving I could tell the service team was operating as a healthy machine. Adding our name to the wait list was a breeze and I could easily track where we were in line through Yelp's app. Once our table was ready, the host took our temperatures before leading us to a nice picnic-style table in the back. Since it was our first time, he delivered a succinct and helpful overview of the menu items and named the server who would be taking care of us.

It didn't take long for us to choose our plates:
Marufuku bites
Kakuni bowl
Hakata tonkotsu deluxe

Bravo! I savored every bite of succulent pork, whether it be sandwiched between two fluffy buns or marinating in mouth-watering broth.

The buns were such a fun starter I wanted a dozen to take home for later. The filling was evenly distributed and I loved whatever sauce sat drizzled on top. I ordered my ramen medium but requested extra spicy on the side and it was perfect. The noodles were soft and tender, the pork melted in my mouth with every bite and the menu description of a "rich" broth didn't disappoint.

Another touch I appreciated were the dishes; each and every bowl / plate / sauce dish was beautiful! Stylish pottery serving up slices of savory heaven in a clean, socially distanced space was exactly what I needed on this Saturday.

Will be back and definitely a new go-to recommendation!<//text><Resp>None<//Resp>< userid>

< Review>
Note on the spicy levels:
1. Mild is with a hint of spice, good for the first-timers.
2. Medium is okay, it's closer to mild in other place.
3. Spicy is the level for those who enjoy the 'bite'.

Awesome staff here, everyone is friendly and very accommodating.

Initially tried to come on Tue, found out last minute, they're close Mon-Tue. Stopped by on Wed, tried the pork ramen... yum!!! Owner even responded to my 5-star post without review. This is a personal level of attention is what separates the great business from the rest. :)

Fast forward to today... my co-worker and I have decided after our lunch yesterday that we'd be back. So we did! And we tried the chicken ramen, which I like even better.

Two 5-star days on the row. I'll definitely be back. Maybe tomorrow? :)</Review>

<Rating>5<//Rating><text>We have been waiting for Marufuku to open since a few months ago and last night it opened, yay! Not only is Marufuku one of the top ramen places in the Bay Area, it's special because it was our first date <3

Having had plenty of Orenchi in the past few months and not much other ramen, we have forgotten what really special ramen tastes like. The tonkotsu broth was rich, savory, and flavorful. It's a more intense flavor than other tonkotsu ramen I've had. The chicken paitan was less intense but has a rich chicken flavor. It's definitely the lighter of the two broths. < Text>
I took my truck here and got the five year warranty paint job.  I should have taken the time to write this review then.  What a mistake that was.

Over spray was everywhere.  Lights, all trim & moldings, bed liner, springs, shocks, frame rails, fuel lines, etc etc.  They painted my electric AMP side steps and even got white paint on my interior!  I had a deadline to be elsewhere so had to bring the truck back to get it fixed.

Three years later the paint is flaking off near every piece of trim, fender wells, bumpers around the doors and much more.  They are so horrid I won't go back there regardless the warranty.  I have a lot more photos but these should give you the idea.

Don't Go MAACO - I should have known better......< /Text>

<review>Decided to try this place out as it's been saved on my map for a hot minute. I actually got 3 breakfast sandwiches as well as these donuts but we ate them too fast lol. So of those sandwiches we got a ham and bacon with egg and cheese on a plain bagel, sausage with egg and cheese on a croissant, bacon with egg and cheese on a croissant. We also got a dozen donuts, 2 apple fritters, and some apple juice from the fridge. My sandwich (sausage, egg, & cheese) was delicious. I finished it before realizing I didnt get a photo. I think the quality of the croissant really carried it because you could taste the croissant in every bite. The sausage tasted really good too. My 7 year old also enjoyed his bacon, egg, and cheese. My husband said his plain bagel was very basic. His said his was good, but it wasn't anything special. We were quite full after the sandwiches but managed to save room for the apple fritters. They were pretty good but still just apple fritters. I dont know about them being worth $2.50 each, I've definitely had same quality for less. The people running the shop were super nice though I'm pretty sure they over charged me a few bucks but its whatever. I wasn't given an itemized receipt to confirm. Overall, I'd definitely go back for another breakfast sandwich, the donuts are good, and they're clearly popular as customers kept coming in while I was there. I took my girlfriend on this date as we had never been on one before and being blown away from the experience is an understatement. It is certainly an experience I recommend everyone to try at least once in their life!

Although the experience is worthy of five stars, I would say that it's a distant second to the experience and professionalism of our Pilot, Terry Frost. The man was enthusiastic, kept things light hearted, and was knowledgeable of all the history of San Diego's landmarks. Even being born and raised in San Diego, I learned so much and Terry's professionalism pushed the experience over the edge to be worthy of going back for more than once! 10/10 without a doubt! Thanks Terry and the CH team!

< Review>
What an amazing experience! We took flight with pilot Terry Frost to celebrate our anniversary. From start to finish the experience was wonderful. I booked online, which was a breeze, you are able to see all the flight packages they offer, where they fly and what the price is. After booking,I received an email confirmation and a second confirmation the day before our flight as a reminder. When we arrived they had a table set up with chocolates and champagne, rose petals were scattered on the table as well. The ladies at the front checking us in were welcoming and advised us our pilot was checking the helicopter and would be right in. Terry came in and introduced himself and asked if we had flown previously and had any questions. He served us some champagne and then off to do some final checks. We were taken to the copter in a golf cart and given some safety info, then with champagne in hand we were off. It's no secret San Diego is a beautiful city -to see it from another perspective and get a sweeping view of the cliffs at Torrey Pines, fly over our world famous zoo and see Padres stadium from high above was a truly amazing experience. Thank you Terry for your professionalism, charm and knowledge. You made our experience wonderful! We will be back :)</Review>

< text>
My grandfather turned 94 recently, and he told us that he had never been in a helicopter.  He was a pilot before WWII and has always been an aviation enthusiast.  My sister and I decided to take him on a tour around San Diego.  We chose to use Corporate Helicopters' services.

The staff at Corporate Helicopters was professional and friendly.  After a short safety briefing, we were on our way.  Our pilot was skilled with her aircraft and knowledgeable of the San Diego area.  She flew us over many of the coastal area's most notable landmarks.

We could not be more pleased with our experiences at Corporate Helicopters and I will gladly recommend them to anyone looking to go up in the air in the San Diego area.<//text>

< Review>
Fantastic!!!! I have gone on helicopter trips only 3 times in my lifetime (I am 53). At 17yrs from Las Vegas through the Grand Canyon with my parents, and then 2 years ago over Manhattan with my daughter.
Now, what this trip did not have the same in sights to offer, but it sure was compensated by the service and flight experience.  Very quaint, very friendly.  San Diego and its coast are beautiful.  The ground staff and the pilot just fantastic.  Unlike the "commercial" feeling of the other trips, this one is like going on a flight with your friend who is the pilot.

Corporate Helis is not rated 4.9 of 5 on google for no reason.  I shall come back to take their longer distance Mexico trips as well.
A grand experience! And I do travel the world!< /Review>

<user_id>110515721443775173444<//user_id><user_name>Tom Jarvis<//user_name><date>1518925162873</date>< rating>
5<//rating>
< Review>
WOW!!  What a wonderful experience with Corporate Helicopters.  I first learned about this company on FOX News when Heather, Fox Reporter, was interviewing one of Corporate Helicopter's Pilots, Peter.  It was a great interview and from this exposure I decided to go to their location and check it out.  Upon arriving I met Jesse, Flight Coordinator, who booked my Valentine Flight.  I was excited that I had an opportunity to pick and reserve a time on Valentine's Day since they are so popular they book up quickly.  Once we arrived we were met by Jesse, and Mandy, Operations Manager, who is so extremely nice and fun to talk to.  Mandy offered us some champagne and handed my wife some roses and then introduced us to Amanda, who gave us a tutorial on our flight.  Amanda then drove us out to the flight deck area via a golf cart and we boarded this very nice Helicopter which is made in Torrance California.  It is a beautiful Helicopter that sits four people counting the Pilot.  Our Pilot turned out to be Peter who was in the interview with Heather.  The flight was smooth quite and our Pilot, Peter, was superb.  We went from Montgomery Field to north of Mt. Soledad, north of Torrey Pines and looped back along the coast at about 1,000 feet.  As we went over the ocean we spotted a California Gray Whale, the water was so clear and the whale was right below us.  The flight hugged the coast line down to Mission Beach over Sea World, then south to San Diego Bay, down to the Coronado Bridge, circle around downtown and over Petco Park and back to Montgomery Field.  It was such a beautiful flight and Peter explained so many things throughout the flight that made the trip that much more interesting.  I highly recommend you take the time to check out Corporate Helicopters and you too will find yourself booking a flight that will leave you with sense of joy and satisfaction and a true thrill.  Very awesome!!!<//Review>

<review>June 2020 update: Campgrounds are open, though many of their sites seem to be on hill/slope terrain. There is a road that goes around the entire lake/one lane 2 way traffic. Asked staff what's the best time to beat the crowds, arrive at 7-8am for a good spot. No safe walking trail for hikers at this lake. Not alot of shade by entire lake shore, bring umbrellas/canopy. Bathrooms with flush toilets with sinks dispersed through out the lake, they are in horrid condition due to mass amounts of crowds. Make sure to read posted signs to avoid strictly enforced ticketing my staff/sherrifs.  Parking is free if you park outside designated parking lots, some parking by boat launch but must pay. Water is warm, too many boats and swimmers for peaceful fishing during the summer, limited fishing spots. Unfortunately someone drowned during our visit, water has strong currents (designated swim area seems safer for children with calm currents) becareful and have fun everyone!< /review>< Rating>
